{"id":"8ee40cbb-a2e5-43b1-b8a8-6c94ee3b9b3b","identifier":"FRG-206","title":"Bug: Characters never talk to each other","description":"AIEngine.\\_applyDecision only handles move/interact/idle — there is no talk action. Characters never approach each other for conversation.

## What exists

* AIEngine.\\_requestDecision builds a prompt with nearby objects, but NOT nearby characters
* The action choices in the prompt are: move, interact, idle
* Character has: currentDialogue, dialogueTimer, pendingSpeech properties
* SimulationEngine already handles pendingSpeech in its update loop

## Implementation

1. In AIEngine.\\_requestDecision: add nearby characters to the prompt context (name, position, current action)
2. Add 'talk' as a fourth action choice in the user prompt:
   { \"action\": \"talk\", \"targetCharacter\": \"character_name\", \"dialogue\": \"...\", \"description\": \"...\" }
3. In AIEngine.\\_applyDecision: add 'talk' case
   * Find target character by name
   * Walk Character A to adjacent tile of Character B (use findAdjacentWalkable)
   * Set Character A's dialogue
   * Set Character B's pendingSpeech to a contextual response (can be from the AI response or a simple acknowledgment)
4. Add conversation events to SimulationEngine.pendingEvents so the debug event log captures them

## Dependencies

* Depends on FRG-218 (AIEngine wired into debug page) to test on debug page
* Can be developed against main page first if needed

## Acceptance

* AI prompt includes nearby characters as context
* Characters occasionally choose 'talk' action targeting another character
* Character A walks to Character B and speaks
* Character B responds with dialogue

     1→/**
     2→ * AIEngine.js — LLM-driven decision engine.
     3→ *
     4→ * When `endpoint` is null (default) the engine is disabled and characters
     5→ * fall back to random wander controlled by SimulationEngine.
     6→ *
     7→ * To enable, pass an endpoint URL and optionally an API key:
     8→ *   new AIEngine({ endpoint: 'https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages', apiKey: '...' })
     9→ *
    10→ * The engine polls each character independently on a configurable interval.
    11→ * Responses are expected as JSON with this shape:
    12→ *   { "action": "move|interact|idle",
    13→ *     "targetId": "object_id",          // for interact
    14→ *     "targetTile": { "tx": 5, "ty": 9 }, // for move
    15→ *     "dialogue": "optional speech",
    16→ *     "description": "what the character is doing" }
    17→ */
    18→
    19→export class AIEngine {
    20→  /**
    21→   * @param {object}  [config]
    22→   * @param {string}  [config.endpoint]            - full URL of LLM API endpoint
    23→   * @param {string}  [config.apiKey]              - bearer token / API key
    24→   * @param {string}  [config.model]               - model ID (for Anthropic-style APIs)
    25→   * @param {number}  [config.decisionIntervalMs]  - ms between decisions per char (default 30 000)
    26→   */
    27→  constructor(config = {}) {
    28→    this.endpoint           = config.endpoint           || null;
    29→    this.apiKey             = config.apiKey             || null;
    30→    this.model              = config.model              || 'claude-sonnet-4-6';
    31→    this.decisionIntervalMs = config.decisionIntervalMs || 30_000;
    32→    this.onDecision         = config.onDecision         || null;
    33→
    34→    this.enabled = !!this.endpoint;
    35→
    36→    // Per-character countdown timers  { name → ms until next decision }
    37→    this._timers = new Map();
    38→    // Prevent overlapping requests  { name → true }
    39→    this._pending = new Set();
    40→  }
    41→
    42→  // ── Called by SimulationEngine each frame ─────────────────────────────────
    43→
    44→  update(deltaMs, characters, objects, simState) {
    45→    if (!this.enabled) return;
    46→
    47→    for (const char of characters) {
    48→      let t = this._timers.get(char.name) ?? 0;
    49→      t -= deltaMs;
    50→
    51→      // Don't make decisions while character is held at an object; let the
    52→      // timer keep ticking so the cooldown UI stays accurate.
    53→      if (t <= 0 && !this._pending.has(char.name) && char.action !== 'interacting') {
    54→        this._timers.set(char.name, this.decisionIntervalMs);
    55→        this._requestDecision(char, objects, simState);
    56→      } else {
    57→        this._timers.set(char.name, t);
    58→      }
    59→    }
    60→  }
    61→
    62→  // ── Internal ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    63→
    64→  async _requestDecision(character, objects, simState) {
    65→    this._pending.add(character.name);
    66→
    67→    try {
    68→      const nearbyObjects = objects
    69→        .filter(obj => {
    70→          const dx = obj.tx - character.tx;
    71→          const dy = obj.ty - character.ty;
    72→          return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= 8;
    73→        })
    74→        .map(o => ({ id: o.id, label: o.label, state: o.state }));
    75→
    76→      const systemPrompt =
    77→        `You are ${character.label}, a character in a cosy Japanese home simulation. ` +
    78→        `Decide what to do next based on your mood (${character.mood}/100) and energy (${character.energy}/100). ` +
    79→        `Reply ONLY with valid JSON — no markdown fences, no extra text.`;
    80→
    81→      const userPrompt =
    82→        `Sim time: ${simState.timeString}. ` +
    83→        `You are at tile (${Math.round(character.tx)}, ${Math.round(character.ty)}). ` +
    84→        `Current action: ${character.action}. ` +
    85→        `Nearby objects: ${JSON.stringify(nearbyObjects)}. ` +
    86→        `Choose one action:
` +
    87→        `  { "action": "move",     "targetTile": {"tx": N, "ty": N}, "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }
` +
    88→        `  { "action": "interact", "targetId": "object_id",          "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }
` +
    89→        `  { "action": "idle",                                        "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }`;
    90→
    91→      const headers = { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' };
    92→
    93→      // Build body — compatible with Anthropic Messages API shape by default;
    94→      // swap for OpenAI chat completions if needed by changing endpoint.
    95→      const body = JSON.stringify({
    96→        model: this.model,
    97→        max_tokens: 256,
    98→        system: systemPrompt,
    99→        messages: [{ role: 'user', content: userPrompt }],
   100→      });
   101→
   102→      const res = await fetch(this.endpoint, { method: 'POST', headers, body });
   103→
   104→      if (!res.ok) {
   105→        console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}: HTTP ${res.status}`);
   106→        return;
   107→      }
   108→
   109→      const data = await res.json();
   110→
   111→      // Extract text from Anthropic-style response; fall back to OpenAI style
   112→      let text = data?.content?.[0]?.text     // Anthropic
   113→              ?? data?.choices?.[0]?.message?.content // OpenAI
   114→              ?? null;
   115→
   116→      if (!text) {
   117→        console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}: unrecognised response shape`, data);
   118→        return;
   119→      }
   120→
   121→      const decision = JSON.parse(text);
   122→      this._applyDecision(character, decision, objects, simState);
   123→    } catch (err) {
   124→      console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}:`, err);
   125→    } finally {
   126→      this._pending.delete(character.name);
   127→    }
   128→  }
   129→
   130→  _applyDecision(character, decision, objects, simState) {
   131→    if (!decision?.action) return;
   132→
   133→    switch (decision.action) {
   134→      case 'move':
   135→        if (decision.targetTile) {
   136→          character.moveTo(decision.targetTile.tx, decision.targetTile.ty);
   137→        }
   138→        break;
   139→
   140→      case 'interact': {
   141→        const obj = objects.find(o => o.id === decision.targetId);
   142→        if (obj) {
   143→          // Walk to an adjacent walkable tile (same pattern as wander engine)
   144→          const adjTile = simState?.findAdjacentWalkable?.(obj.tx, obj.ty);
   145→          if (adjTile && character.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {
   146→            character.targetObjectId = obj.id;
   147→            character.pendingAction  = 'use';
   148→          }
   149→        }
   150→        break;
   151→      }
   152→
   153→      case 'idle':
   154→        // Override wander timer — stay put for one full decision interval
   155→        character.wanderTimer = this.decisionIntervalMs;
   156→        break;
   157→    }
   158→
   159→    if (decision.dialogue) {
   160→      character.currentDialogue = decision.dialogue;
   161→      character.dialogueTimer   = 5000;
   162→    }
   163→
   164→    if (decision.description) {
   165→      console.log(`[${character.label}] ${decision.description}`);
   166→    }
   167→
   168→    if (this.onDecision) {
   169→      this.onDecision(character, decision, objects, simState);
   170→    }
   171→  }
   172→}

✓ TOOL RESULT
SUCCESS 
     1→/**
     2→ * Engine.js — SimulationEngine: manages characters, object state machines, and
     3→ * default random-wander behaviour (with 30% chance of object interaction).
     4→ */
     5→
     6→import { ObjectEngine, OBJECT_DEFS } from './objects.js';
     7→
     8→export class SimulationEngine {
     9→  /**
    10→   * @param {object}      config
    11→   * @param {boolean[][]} config.walkable   - walkable[row][col]
    12→   * @param {number}      config.gridCols
    13→   * @param {number}      config.gridRows
    14→   * @param {object}      [config.aiEngine] - AIEngine instance (optional)
    15→   */
    16→  constructor(config = {}) {
    17→    this.walkable  = config.walkable  || [];
    18→    this.gridCols  = config.gridCols  || 19;
    19→    this.gridRows  = config.gridRows  || 13;
    20→    this.aiEngine  = config.aiEngine  || null;
    21→
    22→    this.characters = [];
    23→
    24→    // Object state machine engine — pre-loaded with Japanese Home objects
    25→    this.objectEngine = new ObjectEngine();
    26→    this.objectEngine.addObjects(OBJECT_DEFS);
    27→
    28→    // Events queued for scene to consume (emoji floats, etc.)
    29→    this.pendingEvents = [];
    30→
    31→    // Sim clock — starts at 08:00 AM game-time
    32→    this.simTimeMs = 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
    33→    // 1 real second = 60 sim seconds  (1 real min = 1 sim hour)
    34→    this.simSpeed  = 60;
    35→
    36→    // Cache walkable tiles list (built lazily)
    37→    this._walkableTiles = null;
    38→  }
    39→
    40→  addCharacter(char) {
    41→    this.characters.push(char);
    42→  }
    43→
    44→  // ── Main update loop ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    45→
    46→  update(deltaMs) {
    47→    // Advance sim clock
    48→    this.simTimeMs += deltaMs * this.simSpeed;
    49→
    50→    // Optional AI decisions — pass live object list so AI sees current states
    51→    if (this.aiEngine) {
    52→      this.aiEngine.update(deltaMs, this.characters, this.objectEngine.getAll(), {
    53→        timeString: this.getSimTimeString(),
    54→        findAdjacentWalkable: this._findAdjacentWalkable.bind(this),
    55→      });
    56→    }
    57→
    58→    // Tick object state machines; collect auto-transition events
    59→    const objEvents = this.objectEngine.tick(deltaMs);
    60→    for (const ev of objEvents) {
    61→      if (ev.emoji) this.pendingEvents.push(ev);
    62→    }
    63→
    64→    for (const char of this.characters) {
    65→      // Handle arrival: character reached target object tile
    66→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.targetObjectId) {
    67→        this._handleObjectArrival(char);
    68→      }
    69→
    70→      // Trigger random wander (or object visit) when idle and timer expired
    71→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.wanderTimer <= 0) {
    72→        this._doWander(char);
    73→      }
    74→
    75→      // Tick speech timer — fire a random line when it expires
    76→      if (char.dialogue.length > 0 && char.pendingSpeech === null) {
    77→        char.speechTimer -= deltaMs;
    78→        if (char.speechTimer <= 0) {
    79→          const idx = Math.floor(Math.random() * char.dialogue.length);
    80→          char.pendingSpeech = char.dialogue[idx];
    81→          char.speechTimer   = 20000 + Math.random() * 20000; // reset 20–40 s
    82→        }
    83→      }
    84→
    85→      // Per-character update (movement, animations, sprite sync)
    86→      char.update(deltaMs);
    87→    }
    88→  }
    89→
    90→  // ── Object interaction ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    91→
    92→  /**
    93→   * Called when a character arrives at an object's adjacent tile.
    94→   * Fires the 'use' transition and puts the character into 'interacting' state.
    95→   */
    96→  _handleObjectArrival(char) {
    97→    const event = this.objectEngine.interact(char.targetObjectId, char.pendingAction || 'use');
    98→
    99→    if (event) {
   100→      const obj = this.objectEngine.getById(char.targetObjectId);
   101→
   102→      // Hold the character for the full auto_next duration if the new state has one;
   103→      // otherwise fall back to the object's generic interactMs.
   104→      let holdMs = obj ? obj.interactMs : 8000;
   105→      if (obj && event.state) {
   106→        const stateDef = obj.states[event.state];
   107→        if (stateDef?.auto_next?.after) {
   108→          holdMs = stateDef.auto_next.after * 1000;
   109→        }
   110→      }
   111→
   112→      char.startInteraction(char.targetObjectId, holdMs);
   113→
   114→      if (event.speech) {
   115→        char.pendingSpeech = event.speech;
   116→      }
   117→
   118→      if (event.emoji) {
   119→        this.pendingEvents.push(event);
   120→      }
   121→    }
   122→    // Always clear targeting so we don't re-fire on next idle frame
   123→    char.targetObjectId = null;
   124→    char.pendingAction  = null;
   125→  }
   126→
   127→  // ── Wander ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   128→
   129→  _doWander(char) {
   130→    // 30% chance: walk to a random interactive object instead of wandering freely
   131→    if (Math.random() < 0.3) {
   132→      const objects = this.objectEngine.getAll();
   133→      if (objects.length > 0) {
   134→        // Shuffle and try each until one yields a reachable adjacent tile
   135→        const shuffled = objects.slice().sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5);
   136→        for (const obj of shuffled) {
   137→          const tile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(obj.tx, obj.ty);
   138→          if (tile && char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty)) {
   139→            char.targetObjectId = obj.id;
   140→            char.pendingAction  = 'use';
   141→            return;
   142→          }
   143→        }
   144→        // All objects unreachable — fall through to random wander
   145→      }
   146→    }
   147→
   148→    // Random walkable tile
   149→    const tiles = this._getWalkableTiles();
   150→    if (tiles.length === 0) {
   151→      char.wanderTimer = 2000;
   152→      return;
   153→    }
   154→
   155→    const cx = Math.round(char.tx);
   156→    const cy = Math.round(char.ty);
   157→
   158→    let moved = false;
   159→    for (let attempt = 0; attempt < 15; attempt++) {
   160→      const tile = tiles[Math.floor(Math.random() * tiles.length)];
   161→      if (tile.tx === cx && tile.ty === cy) continue;
   162→      moved = char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty);
   163→      if (moved) break;
   164→    }
   165→
   166→    if (!moved) {
   167→      char.wanderTimer = 2000;
   168→    }
   169→  }
   170→
   171→  /**
   172→   * Return the first walkable tile cardinally adjacent to (tx, ty), or null.
   173→   */
   174→  _findAdjacentWalkable(tx, ty) {
   175→    const dirs = [
   176→      { tx, ty: ty - 1 },
   177→      { tx, ty: ty + 1 },
   178→      { tx: tx - 1, ty },
   179→      { tx: tx + 1, ty },
   180→    ];
   181→    for (const d of dirs) {
   182→      if (d.tx >= 0 && d.tx < this.gridCols && d.ty >= 0 && d.ty < this.gridRows) {
   183→        if (this.walkable[d.ty]?.[d.tx]) return d;
   184→      }
   185→    }
   186→    return null;
   187→  }
   188→
   189→  _getWalkableTiles() {
   190→    if (this._walkableTiles) return this._walkableTiles;
   191→    const tiles = [];
   192→    for (let row = 0; row < this.gridRows; row++) {
   193→      for (let col = 0; col < this.gridCols; col++) {
   194→        if (this.walkable[row]?.[col]) tiles.push({ tx: col, ty: row });
   195→      }
   196→    }
   197→    this._walkableTiles = tiles;
   198→    return tiles;
   199→  }
   200→
   201→  // ── Sim clock ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   202→
   203→  getSimTimeString() {
   204→    const totalSec = Math.floor(this.simTimeMs / 1000);
   205→    const hours    = Math.floor(totalSec / 3600) % 24;
   206→    const minutes  = Math.floor((totalSec % 3600) / 60);
   207→    const ampm     = hours >= 12 ? 'PM' : 'AM';
   208→    const h        = hours % 12 || 12;
   209→    return `${h}:${String(minutes).padStart(2, '0')} ${ampm}`;
   210→  }
   211→}

     1→/**
     2→ * Character.js — tile-based character with A* pathfinding and state machine.
     3→ * Pure JS, no Phaser dependency. Sprite/label references are set externally.
     4→ */
     5→
     6→const TILE_SIZE = 48;
     7→
     8→// ─── A* pathfinding ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
     9→
    10→function heuristic(ax, ay, bx, by) {
    11→  return Math.abs(ax - bx) + Math.abs(ay - by);
    12→}
    13→
    14→/**
    15→ * Find a path from (startX, startY) to (goalX, goalY) on a walkable grid.
    16→ * @param {boolean[][]} walkable  - walkable[row][col]
    17→ * @param {number} cols
    18→ * @param {number} rows
    19→ * @returns {Array<{tx,ty}>|null}  - list of steps NOT including start; null if no path
    20→ */
    21→function findPath(walkable, cols, rows, startX, startY, goalX, goalY) {
    22→  if (startX === goalX && startY === goalY) return [];
    23→  if (!walkable[startY]?.[startX] || !walkable[goalY]?.[goalX]) return null;
    24→
    25→  const key = (x, y) => x * 1000 + y;
    26→
    27→  const open = new Map();
    28→  const closed = new Set();
    29→
    30→  const startNode = { x: startX, y: startY, g: 0, h: heuristic(startX, startY, goalX, goalY), parent: null };
    31→  open.set(key(startX, startY), startNode);
    32→
    33→  while (open.size > 0) {
    34→    // Pick node with lowest f = g + h
    35→    let current = null;
    36→    for (const node of open.values()) {
    37→      if (!current || node.g + node.h < current.g + current.h) current = node;
    38→    }
    39→
    40→    if (current.x === goalX && current.y === goalY) {
    41→      // Reconstruct path
    42→      const path = [];
    43→      let node = current;
    44→      while (node.parent) {
    45→        path.unshift({ tx: node.x, ty: node.y });
    46→        node = node.parent;
    47→      }
    48→      return path;
    49→    }
    50→
    51→    open.delete(key(current.x, current.y));
    52→    closed.add(key(current.x, current.y));
    53→
    54→    const neighbors = [
    55→      { x: current.x + 1, y: current.y },
    56→      { x: current.x - 1, y: current.y },
    57→      { x: current.x,     y: current.y + 1 },
    58→      { x: current.x,     y: current.y - 1 },
    59→    ];
    60→
    61→    for (const n of neighbors) {
    62→      if (n.x < 0 || n.x >= cols || n.y < 0 || n.y >= rows) continue;
    63→      if (!walkable[n.y]?.[n.x]) continue;
    64→      if (closed.has(key(n.x, n.y))) continue;
    65→
    66→      const g = current.g + 1;
    67→      const existing = open.get(key(n.x, n.y));
    68→      if (existing) {
    69→        if (g < existing.g) {
    70→          existing.g = g;
    71→          existing.parent = current;
    72→        }
    73→      } else {
    74→        open.set(key(n.x, n.y), {
    75→          x: n.x, y: n.y,
    76→          g, h: heuristic(n.x, n.y, goalX, goalY),
    77→          parent: current,
    78→        });
    79→      }
    80→    }
    81→  }
    82→
    83→  return null; // no path
    84→}
    85→
    86→// ─── Character ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    87→
    88→export class Character {
    89→  /**
    90→   * @param {object} config
    91→   * @param {string}   config.name        - sprite key prefix (e.g. 'Amelia')
    92→   * @param {string}   config.label       - display name (e.g. 'Maple')
    93→   * @param {number}   config.tx          - starting tile X
    94→   * @param {number}   config.ty          - starting tile Y
    95→   * @param {boolean[][]} config.walkable - walkable grid [row][col]
    96→   * @param {number}   config.gridCols
    97→   * @param {number}   config.gridRows
    98→   * @param {object}   [config.sprite]    - Phaser sprite (set after construction)
    99→   * @param {object}   [config.nameLabel] - Phaser Text object
   100→   * @param {number}   [config.moveSpeed] - tiles per second (default 2)
   101→   */
   102→  constructor(config) {
   103→    this.name      = config.name;
   104→    this.label     = config.label;
   105→    this.sprite    = config.sprite    || null;
   106→    this.nameLabel = config.nameLabel || null;
   107→
   108→    this.tx     = config.tx;
   109→    this.ty     = config.ty;
   110→    this.prevTx = config.tx;
   111→    this.prevTy = config.ty;
   112→
   113→    this.path        = [];
   114→    this.moveProgress = 0;
   115→    this.moveSpeed   = config.moveSpeed || 2; // tiles/sec
   116→
   117→    // State: 'idle' | 'walking' | 'interacting'
   118→    this.action = 'idle';
   119→    this.facing = 'down';
   120→
   121→    // Wander: timer counts DOWN; engine starts wander when <= 0
   122→    this.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000; // 3–8 s
   123→
   124→    // Interaction
   125→    this.interactTimer    = 0;
   126→    this.interactTimerMax = 0; // initial duration; used by UI for progress bar
   127→    this.interactTarget   = null;
   128→
   129→    // Personality stats (0–100)
   130→    this.mood   = 100;
   131→    this.energy = 100;
   132→
   133→    // Optional dialogue driven by AI
   134→    this.currentDialogue = null;
   135→    this.dialogueTimer   = 0;
   136→
   137→    // Preset dialogue lines (used for random speech bubbles)
   138→    this.dialogue     = config.dialogue || [];
   139→    // Counts down; when it hits 0 Engine sets pendingSpeech
   140→    this.speechTimer  = 20000 + Math.random() * 20000; // 20–40 s
   141→    // Scene reads this each frame and shows a bubble, then clears it
   142→    this.pendingSpeech = null;
   143→
   144→    this.walkable  = config.walkable;
   145→    this.gridCols  = config.gridCols;
   146→    this.gridRows  = config.gridRows;
   147→
   148→    // Object interaction targeting — set by engine, cleared on arrival
   149→    this.targetObjectId = null;
   150→    this.pendingAction  = null;
   151→  }
   152→
   153→  // ── Computed pixel position (Phaser setOrigin(0.5, 1) — feet at py) ─────────
   154→
   155→  get px() {
   156→    if (this.path.length === 0) {
   157→      return this.tx * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2;
   158→    }
   159→    const next = this.path[0];
   160→    return (this.prevTx + (next.tx - this.prevTx) * this.moveProgress) * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2;
   161→  }
   162→
   163→  get py() {
   164→    if (this.path.length === 0) {
   165→      return (this.ty + 1) * TILE_SIZE;
   166→    }
   167→    const next = this.path[0];
   168→    return (this.prevTy + (next.ty - this.prevTy) * this.moveProgress + 1) * TILE_SIZE;
   169→  }
   170→
   171→  // ── Movement ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   172→
   173→  moveTo(goalTx, goalTy) {
   174→    const sx = Math.round(this.tx);
   175→    const sy = Math.round(this.ty);
   176→    const path = findPath(this.walkable, this.gridCols, this.gridRows, sx, sy, goalTx, goalTy);
   177→
   178→    if (path && path.length > 0) {
   179→      this.path         = path;
   180→      this.prevTx       = sx;
   181→      this.prevTy       = sy;
   182→      this.moveProgress = 0;
   183→      this.action       = 'walking';
   184→
   185→      // Set initial facing from first step
   186→      this._updateFacingFromNextTile();
   187→      this._playWalkAnim();
   188→      return true;
   189→    }
   190→    return false;
   191→  }
   192→
   193→  /** Convenience wrapper — start interaction with a named object. */
   194→  startInteraction(objectId, durationMs) {
   195→    this.startInteract(objectId, durationMs);
   196→  }
   197→
   198→  startInteract(target, durationMs) {
   199→    this.action           = 'interacting';
   200→    this.interactTarget   = target;
   201→    this.interactTimer    = durationMs;
   202→    this.interactTimerMax = durationMs;
   203→    if (this.sprite) {
   204→      this.sprite.play(`${this.name}_idle_anim`, true);
   205→    }
   206→  }
   207→
   208→  // ── Per-frame update ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   209→
   210→  update(deltaMs) {
   211→    if (this.action === 'walking' && this.path.length > 0) {
   212→      const tileDurationMs = 1000 / this.moveSpeed;
   213→      this.moveProgress += deltaMs / tileDurationMs;
   214→
   215→      // Update facing toward next tile in path
   216→      this._updateFacingFromNextTile();
   217→
   218→      // Advance tiles
   219→      while (this.moveProgress >= 1 && this.path.length > 0) {
   220→        this.moveProgress -= 1;
   221→        const arrived = this.path.shift();
   222→        this.prevTx = arrived.tx;
   223→        this.prevTy = arrived.ty;
   224→        this.tx     = arrived.tx;
   225→        this.ty     = arrived.ty;
   226→      }
   227→
   228→      if (this.path.length === 0) {
   229→        this.moveProgress = 0;
   230→        this.action       = 'idle';
   231→        this.wanderTimer  = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   232→        this._playAnim('idle');
   233→      } else {
   234→        this._playWalkAnim();
   235→      }
   236→    } else if (this.action === 'idle') {
   237→      this.wanderTimer -= deltaMs;
   238→    } else if (this.action === 'interacting') {
   239→      this.interactTimer -= deltaMs;
   240→      if (this.interactTimer <= 0) {
   241→        this.action        = 'idle';
   242→        this.interactTarget = null;
   243→        this.wanderTimer   = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   244→        this._playAnim('idle');
   245→      }
   246→    }
   247→
   248→    // Tick dialogue
   249→    if (this.dialogueTimer > 0) {
   250→      this.dialogueTimer -= deltaMs;
   251→      if (this.dialogueTimer <= 0) this.currentDialogue = null;
   252→    }
   253→
   254→    // Sync Phaser sprite
   255→    if (this.sprite) {
   256→      this.sprite.x = this.px;
   257→      this.sprite.y = this.py;
   258→    }
   259→
   260→    if (this.nameLabel && this.sprite) {
   261→      this.nameLabel.setPosition(this.sprite.x, this.sprite.y - 100);
   262→    }
   263→  }
   264→
   265→  // ── Perception ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   266→
   267→  /** Returns objects within `radius` tiles. */
   268→  getPerceivedObjects(objects, radius = 4) {
   269→    return objects.filter(obj => {
   270→      const dx = obj.tx - this.tx;
   271→      const dy = obj.ty - this.ty;
   272→      return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= radius;
   273→    });
   274→  }
   275→
   276→  // ── Animation helpers ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   277→
   278→  _updateFacingFromNextTile() {
   279→    if (this.path.length === 0) return;
   280→    const next = this.path[0];
   281→    const dx   = next.tx - this.tx;
   282→    const dy   = next.ty - this.ty;
   283→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= Math.abs(dy)) {
   284→      this.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'right' : 'left';
   285→    } else {
   286→      this.facing = dy > 0 ? 'down' : 'up';
   287→    }
   288→  }
   289→
   290→  _playAnim(type) {
   291→    if (!this.sprite) return;
   292→    const key = type === 'idle'
   293→      ? `${this.name}_idle_anim`
   294→      : `${this.name}_walk_${this.facing}`;
   295→    if (this.sprite.anims.currentAnim?.key !== key) {
   296→      this.sprite.play(key, true);
   297→    }
   298→    this.sprite.flipX = (type === 'walk' && this.facing === 'left');
   299→  }
   300→
   301→  _playWalkAnim() {
   302→    this._playAnim('walk');
   303→  }
   304→}
   305→

Perfect! I've successfully found and read all three files. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Files Located and Read

### 1. AIEngine.js
**Path:** `/home/gem/project/src/AIEngine.js`

This is an LLM-driven decision engine that enables AI-powered character behavior. Key features:
- Can be disabled (default) or enabled with an API endpoint and optional API key
- Polls each character independently on a configurable interval (default 30 seconds)
- Compatible with both Anthropic and OpenAI-style API responses
- Sends system and user prompts to the LLM with character context (mood, energy, nearby objects)
- Supports three actions: move, interact, and idle
- Handles dialogue and description output from the LLM
- Prevents overlapping requests and skips decisions while character is interacting
- Applies AI decisions by setting movement targets, object interactions, or idle states

### 2. Engine.js (SimulationEngine)
**Path:** `/home/gem/project/src/Engine.js`

This is the core simulation engine managing characters, objects, and default behavior. Key features:
- Manages a grid-based world with walkable/non-walkable tiles
- Optionally integrates with AIEngine for LLM decisions
- Includes an ObjectEngine for state machine-driven objects (Japanese home objects)
- Implements a sim clock that runs at 60x speed (1 real second = 60 sim seconds)
- Handles random wander behavior with 30% chance of object interaction
- Manages character-object interactions with hold durations
- Has speech/dialogue system with random speech bubbles
- Provides helper methods for pathfinding and adjacent tile checks
- Queues events (emoji floats) for the scene to consume

### 3. Character.js
**Path:** `/home/gem/project/src/Character.js`

This is a tile-based character class with pathfinding and state management. Key features:
- Pure JavaScript implementation (no Phaser core dependency, though can integrate with Phaser sprites)
- Implements A* pathfinding algorithm for grid-based movement
- Three action states: idle, walking, interacting
- Supports sprite animation with directional facing (up, down, left, right)
- Personality stats: mood and energy (0-100)
- Handles dialogue display with timers
- Preset dialogue lines for random speech bubbles
- Object interaction targeting system
- Pixel position computed from tile position with smooth movement interpolation
- Perception system to detect nearby objects within radius

All three files are well-documented with comments explaining their purpose and functionality.

     1→/**
     2→ * AIEngine.js — LLM-driven decision engine.
     3→ *
     4→ * When `endpoint` is null (default) the engine is disabled and characters
     5→ * fall back to random wander controlled by SimulationEngine.
     6→ *
     7→ * To enable, pass an endpoint URL and optionally an API key:
     8→ *   new AIEngine({ endpoint: 'https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages', apiKey: '...' })
     9→ *
    10→ * The engine polls each character independently on a configurable interval.
    11→ * Responses are expected as JSON with this shape:
    12→ *   { "action": "move|interact|idle",
    13→ *     "targetId": "object_id",          // for interact
    14→ *     "targetTile": { "tx": 5, "ty": 9 }, // for move
    15→ *     "dialogue": "optional speech",
    16→ *     "description": "what the character is doing" }
    17→ */
    18→
    19→export class AIEngine {
    20→  /**
    21→   * @param {object}  [config]
    22→   * @param {string}  [config.endpoint]            - full URL of LLM API endpoint
    23→   * @param {string}  [config.apiKey]              - bearer token / API key
    24→   * @param {string}  [config.model]               - model ID (for Anthropic-style APIs)
    25→   * @param {number}  [config.decisionIntervalMs]  - ms between decisions per char (default 30 000)
    26→   */
    27→  constructor(config = {}) {
    28→    this.endpoint           = config.endpoint           || null;
    29→    this.apiKey             = config.apiKey             || null;
    30→    this.model              = config.model              || 'claude-sonnet-4-6';
    31→    this.decisionIntervalMs = config.decisionIntervalMs || 30_000;
    32→    this.onDecision         = config.onDecision         || null;
    33→
    34→    this.enabled = !!this.endpoint;
    35→
    36→    // Per-character countdown timers  { name → ms until next decision }
    37→    this._timers = new Map();
    38→    // Prevent overlapping requests  { name → true }
    39→    this._pending = new Set();
    40→  }
    41→
    42→  // ── Called by SimulationEngine each frame ─────────────────────────────────
    43→
    44→  update(deltaMs, characters, objects, simState) {
    45→    if (!this.enabled) return;
    46→
    47→    for (const char of characters) {
    48→      let t = this._timers.get(char.name) ?? 0;
    49→      t -= deltaMs;
    50→
    51→      // Don't make decisions while character is held at an object; let the
    52→      // timer keep ticking so the cooldown UI stays accurate.
    53→      if (t <= 0 && !this._pending.has(char.name) && char.action !== 'interacting') {
    54→        this._timers.set(char.name, this.decisionIntervalMs);
    55→        this._requestDecision(char, objects, simState);
    56→      } else {
    57→        this._timers.set(char.name, t);
    58→      }
    59→    }
    60→  }
    61→
    62→  // ── Internal ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    63→
    64→  async _requestDecision(character, objects, simState) {
    65→    this._pending.add(character.name);
    66→
    67→    try {
    68→      const nearbyObjects = objects
    69→        .filter(obj => {
    70→          const dx = obj.tx - character.tx;
    71→          const dy = obj.ty - character.ty;
    72→          return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= 8;
    73→        })
    74→        .map(o => ({ id: o.id, label: o.label, state: o.state }));
    75→
    76→      const systemPrompt =
    77→        `You are ${character.label}, a character in a cosy Japanese home simulation. ` +
    78→        `Decide what to do next based on your mood (${character.mood}/100) and energy (${character.energy}/100). ` +
    79→        `Reply ONLY with valid JSON — no markdown fences, no extra text.`;
    80→
    81→      const userPrompt =
    82→        `Sim time: ${simState.timeString}. ` +
    83→        `You are at tile (${Math.round(character.tx)}, ${Math.round(character.ty)}). ` +
    84→        `Current action: ${character.action}. ` +
    85→        `Nearby objects: ${JSON.stringify(nearbyObjects)}. ` +
    86→        `Choose one action:
` +
    87→        `  { "action": "move",     "targetTile": {"tx": N, "ty": N}, "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }
` +
    88→        `  { "action": "interact", "targetId": "object_id",          "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }
` +
    89→        `  { "action": "idle",                                        "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }`;
    90→
    91→      const headers = { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' };
    92→
    93→      // Build body — compatible with Anthropic Messages API shape by default;
    94→      // swap for OpenAI chat completions if needed by changing endpoint.
    95→      const body = JSON.stringify({
    96→        model: this.model,
    97→        max_tokens: 256,
    98→        system: systemPrompt,
    99→        messages: [{ role: 'user', content: userPrompt }],
   100→      });
   101→
   102→      const res = await fetch(this.endpoint, { method: 'POST', headers, body });
   103→
   104→      if (!res.ok) {
   105→        console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}: HTTP ${res.status}`);
   106→        return;
   107→      }
   108→
   109→      const data = await res.json();
   110→
   111→      // Extract text from Anthropic-style response; fall back to OpenAI style
   112→      let text = data?.content?.[0]?.text     // Anthropic
   113→              ?? data?.choices?.[0]?.message?.content // OpenAI
   114→              ?? null;
   115→
   116→      if (!text) {
   117→        console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}: unrecognised response shape`, data);
   118→        return;
   119→      }
   120→
   121→      const decision = JSON.parse(text);
   122→      this._applyDecision(character, decision, objects, simState);
   123→    } catch (err) {
   124→      console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}:`, err);
   125→    } finally {
   126→      this._pending.delete(character.name);
   127→    }
   128→  }
   129→
   130→  _applyDecision(character, decision, objects, simState) {
   131→    if (!decision?.action) return;
   132→
   133→    switch (decision.action) {
   134→      case 'move':
   135→        if (decision.targetTile) {
   136→          character.moveTo(decision.targetTile.tx, decision.targetTile.ty);
   137→        }
   138→        break;
   139→
   140→      case 'interact': {
   141→        const obj = objects.find(o => o.id === decision.targetId);
   142→        if (obj) {
   143→          // Walk to an adjacent walkable tile (same pattern as wander engine)
   144→          const adjTile = simState?.findAdjacentWalkable?.(obj.tx, obj.ty);
   145→          if (adjTile && character.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {
   146→            character.targetObjectId = obj.id;
   147→            character.pendingAction  = 'use';
   148→          }
   149→        }
   150→        break;
   151→      }
   152→
   153→      case 'idle':
   154→        // Override wander timer — stay put for one full decision interval
   155→        character.wanderTimer = this.decisionIntervalMs;
   156→        break;
   157→    }
   158→
   159→    if (decision.dialogue) {
   160→      character.currentDialogue = decision.dialogue;
   161→      character.dialogueTimer   = 5000;
   162→    }
   163→
   164→    if (decision.description) {
   165→      console.log(`[${character.label}] ${decision.description}`);
   166→    }
   167→
   168→    if (this.onDecision) {
   169→      this.onDecision(character, decision, objects, simState);
   170→    }
   171→  }
   172→}

     1→/**
     2→ * Engine.js — SimulationEngine: manages characters, object state machines, and
     3→ * default random-wander behaviour (with 30% chance of object interaction).
     4→ */
     5→
     6→import { ObjectEngine, OBJECT_DEFS } from './objects.js';
     7→
     8→export class SimulationEngine {
     9→  /**
    10→   * @param {object}      config
    11→   * @param {boolean[][]} config.walkable   - walkable[row][col]
    12→   * @param {number}      config.gridCols
    13→   * @param {number}      config.gridRows
    14→   * @param {object}      [config.aiEngine] - AIEngine instance (optional)
    15→   */
    16→  constructor(config = {}) {
    17→    this.walkable  = config.walkable  || [];
    18→    this.gridCols  = config.gridCols  || 19;
    19→    this.gridRows  = config.gridRows  || 13;
    20→    this.aiEngine  = config.aiEngine  || null;
    21→
    22→    this.characters = [];
    23→
    24→    // Object state machine engine — pre-loaded with Japanese Home objects
    25→    this.objectEngine = new ObjectEngine();
    26→    this.objectEngine.addObjects(OBJECT_DEFS);
    27→
    28→    // Events queued for scene to consume (emoji floats, etc.)
    29→    this.pendingEvents = [];
    30→
    31→    // Sim clock — starts at 08:00 AM game-time
    32→    this.simTimeMs = 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
    33→    // 1 real second = 60 sim seconds  (1 real min = 1 sim hour)
    34→    this.simSpeed  = 60;
    35→
    36→    // Cache walkable tiles list (built lazily)
    37→    this._walkableTiles = null;
    38→  }
    39→
    40→  addCharacter(char) {
    41→    this.characters.push(char);
    42→  }
    43→
    44→  // ── Main update loop ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    45→
    46→  update(deltaMs) {
    47→    // Advance sim clock
    48→    this.simTimeMs += deltaMs * this.simSpeed;
    49→
    50→    // Optional AI decisions — pass live object list so AI sees current states
    51→    if (this.aiEngine) {
    52→      this.aiEngine.update(deltaMs, this.characters, this.objectEngine.getAll(), {
    53→        timeString: this.getSimTimeString(),
    54→        findAdjacentWalkable: this._findAdjacentWalkable.bind(this),
    55→      });
    56→    }
    57→
    58→    // Tick object state machines; collect auto-transition events
    59→    const objEvents = this.objectEngine.tick(deltaMs);
    60→    for (const ev of objEvents) {
    61→      if (ev.emoji) this.pendingEvents.push(ev);
    62→    }
    63→
    64→    for (const char of this.characters) {
    65→      // Handle arrival: character reached target object tile
    66→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.targetObjectId) {
    67→        this._handleObjectArrival(char);
    68→      }
    69→
    70→      // Trigger random wander (or object visit) when idle and timer expired
    71→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.wanderTimer <= 0) {
    72→        this._doWander(char);
    73→      }
    74→
    75→      // Tick speech timer — fire a random line when it expires
    76→      if (char.dialogue.length > 0 && char.pendingSpeech === null) {
    77→        char.speechTimer -= deltaMs;
    78→        if (char.speechTimer <= 0) {
    79→          const idx = Math.floor(Math.random() * char.dialogue.length);
    80→          char.pendingSpeech = char.dialogue[idx];
    81→          char.speechTimer   = 20000 + Math.random() * 20000; // reset 20–40 s
    82→        }
    83→      }
    84→
    85→      // Per-character update (movement, animations, sprite sync)
    86→      char.update(deltaMs);
    87→    }
    88→  }
    89→
    90→  // ── Object interaction ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    91→
    92→  /**
    93→   * Called when a character arrives at an object's adjacent tile.
    94→   * Fires the 'use' transition and puts the character into 'interacting' state.
    95→   */
    96→  _handleObjectArrival(char) {
    97→    const event = this.objectEngine.interact(char.targetObjectId, char.pendingAction || 'use');
    98→
    99→    if (event) {
   100→      const obj = this.objectEngine.getById(char.targetObjectId);
   101→
   102→      // Hold the character for the full auto_next duration if the new state has one;
   103→      // otherwise fall back to the object's generic interactMs.
   104→      let holdMs = obj ? obj.interactMs : 8000;
   105→      if (obj && event.state) {
   106→        const stateDef = obj.states[event.state];
   107→        if (stateDef?.auto_next?.after) {
   108→          holdMs = stateDef.auto_next.after * 1000;
   109→        }
   110→      }
   111→
   112→      char.startInteraction(char.targetObjectId, holdMs);
   113→
   114→      if (event.speech) {
   115→        char.pendingSpeech = event.speech;
   116→      }
   117→
   118→      if (event.emoji) {
   119→        this.pendingEvents.push(event);
   120→      }
   121→    }
   122→    // Always clear targeting so we don't re-fire on next idle frame
   123→    char.targetObjectId = null;
   124→    char.pendingAction  = null;
   125→  }
   126→
   127→  // ── Wander ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   128→
   129→  _doWander(char) {
   130→    // 30% chance: walk to a random interactive object instead of wandering freely
   131→    if (Math.random() < 0.3) {
   132→      const objects = this.objectEngine.getAll();
   133→      if (objects.length > 0) {
   134→        // Shuffle and try each until one yields a reachable adjacent tile
   135→        const shuffled = objects.slice().sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5);
   136→        for (const obj of shuffled) {
   137→          const tile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(obj.tx, obj.ty);
   138→          if (tile && char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty)) {
   139→            char.targetObjectId = obj.id;
   140→            char.pendingAction  = 'use';
   141→            return;
   142→          }
   143→        }
   144→        // All objects unreachable — fall through to random wander
   145→      }
   146→    }
   147→
   148→    // Random walkable tile
   149→    const tiles = this._getWalkableTiles();
   150→    if (tiles.length === 0) {
   151→      char.wanderTimer = 2000;
   152→      return;
   153→    }
   154→
   155→    const cx = Math.round(char.tx);
   156→    const cy = Math.round(char.ty);
   157→
   158→    let moved = false;
   159→    for (let attempt = 0; attempt < 15; attempt++) {
   160→      const tile = tiles[Math.floor(Math.random() * tiles.length)];
   161→      if (tile.tx === cx && tile.ty === cy) continue;
   162→      moved = char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty);
   163→      if (moved) break;
   164→    }
   165→
   166→    if (!moved) {
   167→      char.wanderTimer = 2000;
   168→    }
   169→  }
   170→
   171→  /**
   172→   * Return the first walkable tile cardinally adjacent to (tx, ty), or null.
   173→   */
   174→  _findAdjacentWalkable(tx, ty) {
   175→    const dirs = [
   176→      { tx, ty: ty - 1 },
   177→      { tx, ty: ty + 1 },
   178→      { tx: tx - 1, ty },
   179→      { tx: tx + 1, ty },
   180→    ];
   181→    for (const d of dirs) {
   182→      if (d.tx >= 0 && d.tx < this.gridCols && d.ty >= 0 && d.ty < this.gridRows) {
   183→        if (this.walkable[d.ty]?.[d.tx]) return d;
   184→      }
   185→    }
   186→    return null;
   187→  }
   188→
   189→  _getWalkableTiles() {
   190→    if (this._walkableTiles) return this._walkableTiles;
   191→    const tiles = [];
   192→    for (let row = 0; row < this.gridRows; row++) {
   193→      for (let col = 0; col < this.gridCols; col++) {
   194→        if (this.walkable[row]?.[col]) tiles.push({ tx: col, ty: row });
   195→      }
   196→    }
   197→    this._walkableTiles = tiles;
   198→    return tiles;
   199→  }
   200→
   201→  // ── Sim clock ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   202→
   203→  getSimTimeString() {
   204→    const totalSec = Math.floor(this.simTimeMs / 1000);
   205→    const hours    = Math.floor(totalSec / 3600) % 24;
   206→    const minutes  = Math.floor((totalSec % 3600) / 60);
   207→    const ampm     = hours >= 12 ? 'PM' : 'AM';
   208→    const h        = hours % 12 || 12;
   209→    return `${h}:${String(minutes).padStart(2, '0')} ${ampm}`;
   210→  }
   211→}

     1→/**
     2→ * Character.js — tile-based character with A* pathfinding and state machine.
     3→ * Pure JS, no Phaser dependency. Sprite/label references are set externally.
     4→ */
     5→
     6→const TILE_SIZE = 48;
     7→
     8→// ─── A* pathfinding ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
     9→
    10→function heuristic(ax, ay, bx, by) {
    11→  return Math.abs(ax - bx) + Math.abs(ay - by);
    12→}
    13→
    14→/**
    15→ * Find a path from (startX, startY) to (goalX, goalY) on a walkable grid.
    16→ * @param {boolean[][]} walkable  - walkable[row][col]
    17→ * @param {number} cols
    18→ * @param {number} rows
    19→ * @returns {Array<{tx,ty}>|null}  - list of steps NOT including start; null if no path
    20→ */
    21→function findPath(walkable, cols, rows, startX, startY, goalX, goalY) {
    22→  if (startX === goalX && startY === goalY) return [];
    23→  if (!walkable[startY]?.[startX] || !walkable[goalY]?.[goalX]) return null;
    24→
    25→  const key = (x, y) => x * 1000 + y;
    26→
    27→  const open = new Map();
    28→  const closed = new Set();
    29→
    30→  const startNode = { x: startX, y: startY, g: 0, h: heuristic(startX, startY, goalX, goalY), parent: null };
    31→  open.set(key(startX, startY), startNode);
    32→
    33→  while (open.size > 0) {
    34→    // Pick node with lowest f = g + h
    35→    let current = null;
    36→    for (const node of open.values()) {
    37→      if (!current || node.g + node.h < current.g + current.h) current = node;
    38→    }
    39→
    40→    if (current.x === goalX && current.y === goalY) {
    41→      // Reconstruct path
    42→      const path = [];
    43→      let node = current;
    44→      while (node.parent) {
    45→        path.unshift({ tx: node.x, ty: node.y });
    46→        node = node.parent;
    47→      }
    48→      return path;
    49→    }
    50→
    51→    open.delete(key(current.x, current.y));
    52→    closed.add(key(current.x, current.y));
    53→
    54→    const neighbors = [
    55→      { x: current.x + 1, y: current.y },
    56→      { x: current.x - 1, y: current.y },
    57→      { x: current.x,     y: current.y + 1 },
    58→      { x: current.x,     y: current.y - 1 },
    59→    ];
    60→
    61→    for (const n of neighbors) {
    62→      if (n.x < 0 || n.x >= cols || n.y < 0 || n.y >= rows) continue;
    63→      if (!walkable[n.y]?.[n.x]) continue;
    64→      if (closed.has(key(n.x, n.y))) continue;
    65→
    66→      const g = current.g + 1;
    67→      const existing = open.get(key(n.x, n.y));
    68→      if (existing) {
    69→        if (g < existing.g) {
    70→          existing.g = g;
    71→          existing.parent = current;
    72→        }
    73→      } else {
    74→        open.set(key(n.x, n.y), {
    75→          x: n.x, y: n.y,
    76→          g, h: heuristic(n.x, n.y, goalX, goalY),
    77→          parent: current,
    78→        });
    79→      }
    80→    }
    81→  }
    82→
    83→  return null; // no path
    84→}

    86→// ─── Character ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    87→
    88→export class Character {
    89→  /**
    90→   * @param {object} config
    91→   * @param {string}   config.name        - sprite key prefix (e.g. 'Amelia')
    92→   * @param {string}   config.label       - display name (e.g. 'Maple')
    93→   * @param {number}   config.tx          - starting tile X
    94→   * @param {number}   config.ty          - starting tile Y
    95→   * @param {boolean[][]} config.walkable - walkable grid [row][col]
    96→   * @param {number}   config.gridCols
    97→   * @param {number}   config.gridRows
    98→   * @param {object}   [config.sprite]    - Phaser sprite (set after construction)
    99→   * @param {object}   [config.nameLabel] - Phaser Text object
   100→   * @param {number}   [config.moveSpeed] - tiles per second (default 2)
   101→   */
   102→  constructor(config) {
   103→    this.name      = config.name;
   104→    this.label     = config.label;
   105→    this.sprite    = config.sprite    || null;
   106→    this.nameLabel = config.nameLabel || null;
   107→
   108→    this.tx     = config.tx;
   109→    this.ty     = config.ty;
   110→    this.prevTx = config.tx;
   111→    this.prevTy = config.ty;
   112→
   113→    this.path        = [];
   114→    this.moveProgress = 0;
   115→    this.moveSpeed   = config.moveSpeed || 2; // tiles/sec
   116→
   117→    // State: 'idle' | 'walking' | 'interacting'
   118→    this.action = 'idle';
   119→    this.facing = 'down';
   120→
   121→    // Wander: timer counts DOWN; engine starts wander when <= 0
   122→    this.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000; // 3–8 s
   123→
   124→    // Interaction
   125→    this.interactTimer    = 0;
   126→    this.interactTimerMax = 0; // initial duration; used by UI for progress bar
   127→    this.interactTarget   = null;
   128→
   129→    // Personality stats (0–100)
   130→    this.mood   = 100;
   131→    this.energy = 100;
   132→
   133→    // Optional dialogue driven by AI
   134→    this.currentDialogue = null;
   135→    this.dialogueTimer   = 0;
   136→
   137→    // Preset dialogue lines (used for random speech bubbles)
   138→    this.dialogue     = config.dialogue || [];
   139→    // Counts down; when it hits 0 Engine sets pendingSpeech
   140→    this.speechTimer  = 20000 + Math.random() * 20000; // 20–40 s
   141→    // Scene reads this each frame and shows a bubble, then clears it
   142→    this.pendingSpeech = null;
   143→
   144→    this.walkable  = config.walkable;
   145→    this.gridCols  = config.gridCols;
   146→    this.gridRows  = config.gridRows;
   147→
   148→    // Object interaction targeting — set by engine, cleared on arrival
   149→    this.targetObjectId = null;
   150→    this.pendingAction  = null;
   151→  }
   152→
   153→  // ── Computed pixel position (Phaser setOrigin(0.5, 1) — feet at py) ─────────
   154→
   155→  get px() {
   156→    if (this.path.length === 0) {
   157→      return this.tx * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2;
   158→    }
   159→    const next = this.path[0];
   160→    return (this.prevTx + (next.tx - this.prevTx) * this.moveProgress) * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2;
   161→  }
   162→
   163→  get py() {
   164→    if (this.path.length === 0) {
   165→      return (this.ty + 1) * TILE_SIZE;
   166→    }
   167→    const next = this.path[0];
   168→    return (this.prevTy + (next.ty - this.prevTy) * this.moveProgress + 1) * TILE_SIZE;
   169→  }
   170→
   171→  // ── Movement ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   172→
   173→  moveTo(goalTx, goalTy) {
   174→    const sx = Math.round(this.tx);
   175→    const sy = Math.round(this.ty);
   176→    const path = findPath(this.walkable, this.gridCols, this.gridRows, sx, sy, goalTx, goalTy);
   177→
   178→    if (path && path.length > 0) {
   179→      this.path         = path;
   180→      this.prevTx       = sx;
   181→      this.prevTy       = sy;
   182→      this.moveProgress = 0;
   183→      this.action       = 'walking';
   184→
   185→      // Set initial facing from first step
   186→      this._updateFacingFromNextTile();
   187→      this._playWalkAnim();
   188→      return true;
   189→    }
   190→    return false;
   191→  }
   192→
   193→  /** Convenience wrapper — start interaction with a named object. */
   194→  startInteraction(objectId, durationMs) {
   195→    this.startInteract(objectId, durationMs);
   196→  }
   197→
   198→  startInteract(target, durationMs) {
   199→    this.action           = 'interacting';
   200→    this.interactTarget   = target;
   201→    this.interactTimer    = durationMs;
   202→    this.interactTimerMax = durationMs;
   203→    if (this.sprite) {
   204→      this.sprite.play(`${this.name}_idle_anim`, true);
   205→    }
   206→  }
   207→
   208→  // ── Per-frame update ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   209→
   210→  update(deltaMs) {
   211→    if (this.action === 'walking' && this.path.length > 0) {
   212→      const tileDurationMs = 1000 / this.moveSpeed;
   213→      this.moveProgress += deltaMs / tileDurationMs;
   214→
   215→      // Update facing toward next tile in path
   216→      this._updateFacingFromNextTile();
   217→
   218→      // Advance tiles
   219→      while (this.moveProgress >= 1 && this.path.length > 0) {
   220→        this.moveProgress -= 1;
   221→        const arrived = this.path.shift();
   222→        this.prevTx = arrived.tx;
   223→        this.prevTy = arrived.ty;
   224→        this.tx     = arrived.tx;
   225→        this.ty     = arrived.ty;
   226→      }
   227→
   228→      if (this.path.length === 0) {
   229→        this.moveProgress = 0;
   230→        this.action       = 'idle';
   231→        this.wanderTimer  = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   232→        this._playAnim('idle');
   233→      } else {
   234→        this._playWalkAnim();
   235→      }
   236→    } else if (this.action === 'idle') {
   237→      this.wanderTimer -= deltaMs;
   238→    } else if (this.action === 'interacting') {
   239→      this.interactTimer -= deltaMs;
   240→      if (this.interactTimer <= 0) {
   241→        this.action        = 'idle';
   242→        this.interactTarget = null;
   243→        this.wanderTimer   = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   244→        this._playAnim('idle');
   245→      }
   246→    }
   247→
   248→    // Tick dialogue
   249→    if (this.dialogueTimer > 0) {
   250→      this.dialogueTimer -= deltaMs;
   251→      if (this.dialogueTimer <= 0) this.currentDialogue = null;
   252→    }
   253→
   254→    // Sync Phaser sprite
   255→    if (this.sprite) {
   256→      this.sprite.x = this.px;
   257→      this.sprite.y = this.py;
   258→    }
   259→
   260→    if (this.nameLabel && this.sprite) {
   261→      this.nameLabel.setPosition(this.sprite.x, this.sprite.y - 100);
   262→    }
   263→  }
   264→
   265→  // ── Perception ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   266→
   267→  /** Returns objects within `radius` tiles. */
   268→  getPerceivedObjects(objects, radius = 4) {
   269→    return objects.filter(obj => {
   270→      const dx = obj.tx - this.tx;
   271→      const dy = obj.ty - this.ty;
   272→      return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= radius;
   273→    });
   274→  }
   275→
   276→  // ── Animation helpers ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   277→
   278→  _updateFacingFromNextTile() {
   279→    if (this.path.length === 0) return;
   280→    const next = this.path[0];
   281→    const dx   = next.tx - this.tx;
   282→    const dy   = next.ty - this.ty;
   283→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= Math.abs(dy)) {
   284→      this.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'right' : 'left';
   285→    } else {
   286→      this.facing = dy > 0 ? 'down' : 'up';
   287→    }
   288→  }
   289→
   290→  _playAnim(type) {
   291→    if (!this.sprite) return;
   292→    const key = type === 'idle'
   293→      ? `${this.name}_idle_anim`
   294→      : `${this.name}_walk_${this.facing}`;
   295→    if (this.sprite.anims.currentAnim?.key !== key) {
   296→      this.sprite.play(key, true);
   297→    }
   298→    this.sprite.flipX = (type === 'walk' && this.facing === 'left');
   299→  }
   300→
   301→  _playWalkAnim() {
   302→    this._playAnim('walk');
   303→  }
   304→}

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #63
Edit TOOL CALL 
{
  "replace_all": false,
  "file_path": "/home/gem/project/src/AIEngine.js",
  "old_string": "  _applyDecision(character, decision, objects, simState) {\n    if (!decision?.action) return;\n\n    switch (decision.action) {\n      case 'move':\n        if (decision.targetTile) {\n          character.moveTo(decision.targetTile.tx, decision.targetTile.ty);\n        }\n        break;\n\n      case 'interact': {\n        const obj = objects.find(o => o.id === decision.targetId);\n        if (obj) {\n          // Walk to an adjacent walkable tile (same pattern as wander engine)\n          const adjTile = simState?.findAdjacentWalkable?.(obj.tx, obj.ty);\n          if (adjTile && character.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {\n            character.targetObjectId = obj.id;\n            character.pendingAction  = 'use';\n          }\n        }\n        break;\n      }\n\n      case 'idle':\n        // Override wander timer \u2014 stay put for one full decision interval\n        character.wanderTimer = this.decisionIntervalMs;\n        break;\n    }",
  "new_string": "  _applyDecision(character, decision, characters, objects, simState) {\n    if (!decision?.action) return;\n\n    switch (decision.action) {\n      case 'move':\n        if (decision.targetTile) {\n          character.moveTo(decision.targetTile.tx, decision.targetTile.ty);\n        }\n        break;\n\n      case 'interact': {\n        const obj = objects.find(o => o.id === decision.targetId);\n        if (obj) {\n          // Walk to an adjacent walkable tile (same pattern as wander engine)\n          const adjTile = simState?.findAdjacentWalkable?.(obj.tx, obj.ty);\n          if (adjTile && character.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {\n            character.targetObjectId = obj.id;\n            character.pendingAction  = 'use';\n          }\n        }\n        break;\n      }\n\n      case 'idle':\n        // Override wander timer \u2014 stay put for one full decision interval\n        character.wanderTimer = this.decisionIntervalMs;\n        break;\n\n      case 'talk': {\n        const target = characters.find(c => c.name === decision.targetCharacter);\n        if (target) {\n          // Walk Character A to a tile adjacent to Character B\n          const adjTile = simState?.findAdjacentWalkable?.(Math.round(target.tx), Math.round(target.ty));\n          if (adjTile && character.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {\n            // Character B responds when A arrives\n            if (decision.targetDialogue) {\n              target.pendingSpeech = decision.targetDialogue;\n            }\n            // Queue conversation event for the debug log\n            if (simState?.pushEvent) {\n              simState.pushEvent({\n                type: 'conversation',\n                speakerLabel: character.label,\n                targetLabel: target.label,\n                dialogue: decision.dialogue || '',\n                response: decision.targetDialogue || '',\n              });\n            }\n          }\n        }\n        break;\n      }\n    }"
}

USERMESSAGE #74
✓ TOOL RESULT
SUCCESS 
     1→/**
     2→ * AIEngine.js — LLM-driven decision engine.
     3→ *
     4→ * When `endpoint` is null (default) the engine is disabled and characters
     5→ * fall back to random wander controlled by SimulationEngine.
     6→ *
     7→ * To enable, pass an endpoint URL and optionally an API key:
     8→ *   new AIEngine({ endpoint: 'https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages', apiKey: '...' })
     9→ *
    10→ * The engine polls each character independently on a configurable interval.
    11→ * Responses are expected as JSON with this shape:
    12→ *   { "action": "move|interact|idle|talk",
    13→ *     "targetId": "object_id",               // for interact
    14→ *     "targetTile": { "tx": 5, "ty": 9 },    // for move
    15→ *     "targetCharacter": "character_name",   // for talk
    16→ *     "dialogue": "optional speech",
    17→ *     "targetDialogue": "response from target character", // for talk
    18→ *     "description": "what the character is doing" }
    19→ */
    20→
    21→export class AIEngine {
    22→  /**
    23→   * @param {object}  [config]
    24→   * @param {string}  [config.endpoint]            - full URL of LLM API endpoint
    25→   * @param {string}  [config.apiKey]              - bearer token / API key
    26→   * @param {string}  [config.model]               - model ID (for Anthropic-style APIs)
    27→   * @param {number}  [config.decisionIntervalMs]  - ms between decisions per char (default 30 000)
    28→   */
    29→  constructor(config = {}) {
    30→    this.endpoint           = config.endpoint           || null;
    31→    this.apiKey             = config.apiKey             || null;
    32→    this.model              = config.model              || 'claude-sonnet-4-6';
    33→    this.decisionIntervalMs = config.decisionIntervalMs || 30_000;
    34→    this.onDecision         = config.onDecision         || null;
    35→
    36→    this.enabled = !!this.endpoint;
    37→
    38→    // Per-character countdown timers  { name → ms until next decision }
    39→    this._timers = new Map();
    40→    // Prevent overlapping requests  { name → true }
    41→    this._pending = new Set();
    42→  }
    43→
    44→  // ── Called by SimulationEngine each frame ─────────────────────────────────
    45→
    46→  update(deltaMs, characters, objects, simState) {
    47→    if (!this.enabled) return;
    48→
    49→    for (const char of characters) {
    50→      let t = this._timers.get(char.name) ?? 0;
    51→      t -= deltaMs;
    52→
    53→      // Don't make decisions while character is held at an object; let the
    54→      // timer keep ticking so the cooldown UI stays accurate.
    55→      if (t <= 0 && !this._pending.has(char.name) && char.action !== 'interacting') {
    56→        this._timers.set(char.name, this.decisionIntervalMs);
    57→        this._requestDecision(char, characters, objects, simState);
    58→      } else {
    59→        this._timers.set(char.name, t);
    60→      }
    61→    }
    62→  }
    63→
    64→  // ── Internal ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    65→
    66→  async _requestDecision(character, characters, objects, simState) {
    67→    this._pending.add(character.name);
    68→
    69→    try {
    70→      const nearbyObjects = objects
    71→        .filter(obj => {
    72→          const dx = obj.tx - character.tx;
    73→          const dy = obj.ty - character.ty;
    74→          return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= 8;
    75→        })
    76→        .map(o => ({ id: o.id, label: o.label, state: o.state }));
    77→
    78→      const nearbyCharacters = characters
    79→        .filter(c => {
    80→          if (c.name === character.name) return false;
    81→          const dx = c.tx - character.tx;
    82→          const dy = c.ty - character.ty;
    83→          return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= 8;
    84→        })
    85→        .map(c => ({ name: c.name, label: c.label, tx: Math.round(c.tx), ty: Math.round(c.ty), action: c.action }));
    86→
    87→      const systemPrompt =
    88→        `You are ${character.label}, a character in a cosy Japanese home simulation. ` +
    89→        `Decide what to do next based on your mood (${character.mood}/100) and energy (${character.energy}/100). ` +
    90→        `Reply ONLY with valid JSON — no markdown fences, no extra text.`;
    91→
    92→      const userPrompt =
    93→        `Sim time: ${simState.timeString}. ` +
    94→        `You are at tile (${Math.round(character.tx)}, ${Math.round(character.ty)}). ` +
    95→        `Current action: ${character.action}. ` +
    96→        `Nearby objects: ${JSON.stringify(nearbyObjects)}. ` +
    97→        `Nearby characters: ${JSON.stringify(nearbyCharacters)}. ` +
    98→        `Choose one action:
` +
    99→        `  { "action": "move",     "targetTile": {"tx": N, "ty": N}, "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }
` +
   100→        `  { "action": "interact", "targetId": "object_id",          "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }
` +
   101→        `  { "action": "idle",                                        "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }
` +
   102→        `  { "action": "talk",     "targetCharacter": "character_name", "dialogue": "what you say", "targetDialogue": "their response", "description": "..." }`;
   103→
   104→      const headers = { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' };
   105→
   106→      // Build body — compatible with Anthropic Messages API shape by default;
   107→      // swap for OpenAI chat completions if needed by changing endpoint.
   108→      const body = JSON.stringify({
   109→        model: this.model,
   110→        max_tokens: 256,
   111→        system: systemPrompt,
   112→        messages: [{ role: 'user', content: userPrompt }],
   113→      });
   114→
   115→      const res = await fetch(this.endpoint, { method: 'POST', headers, body });
   116→
   117→      if (!res.ok) {
   118→        console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}: HTTP ${res.status}`);
   119→        return;
   120→      }
   121→
   122→      const data = await res.json();
   123→
   124→      // Extract text from Anthropic-style response; fall back to OpenAI style
   125→      let text = data?.content?.[0]?.text     // Anthropic
   126→              ?? data?.choices?.[0]?.message?.content // OpenAI
   127→              ?? null;
   128→
   129→      if (!text) {
   130→        console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}: unrecognised response shape`, data);
   131→        return;
   132→      }
   133→
   134→      const decision = JSON.parse(text);
   135→      this._applyDecision(character, decision, characters, objects, simState);
   136→    } catch (err) {
   137→      console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}:`, err);
   138→    } finally {
   139→      this._pending.delete(character.name);
   140→    }
   141→  }
   142→
   143→  _applyDecision(character, decision, characters, objects, simState) {
   144→    if (!decision?.action) return;
   145→
   146→    switch (decision.action) {
   147→      case 'move':
   148→        if (decision.targetTile) {
   149→          character.moveTo(decision.targetTile.tx, decision.targetTile.ty);
   150→        }
   151→        break;
   152→
   153→      case 'interact': {
   154→        const obj = objects.find(o => o.id === decision.targetId);
   155→        if (obj) {
   156→          // Walk to an adjacent walkable tile (same pattern as wander engine)
   157→          const adjTile = simState?.findAdjacentWalkable?.(obj.tx, obj.ty);
   158→          if (adjTile && character.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {
   159→            character.targetObjectId = obj.id;
   160→            character.pendingAction  = 'use';
   161→          }
   162→        }
   163→        break;
   164→      }
   165→
   166→      case 'idle':
   167→        // Override wander timer — stay put for one full decision interval
   168→        character.wanderTimer = this.decisionIntervalMs;
   169→        break;
   170→
   171→      case 'talk': {
   172→        const target = characters.find(c => c.name === decision.targetCharacter);
   173→        if (target) {
   174→          // Walk Character A to a tile adjacent to Character B
   175→          const adjTile = simState?.findAdjacentWalkable?.(Math.round(target.tx), Math.round(target.ty));
   176→          if (adjTile && character.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {
   177→            // Character B responds when A arrives
   178→            if (decision.targetDialogue) {
   179→              target.pendingSpeech = decision.targetDialogue;
   180→            }
   181→            // Queue conversation event for the debug log
   182→            if (simState?.pushEvent) {
   183→              simState.pushEvent({
   184→                type: 'conversation',
   185→                speakerLabel: character.label,
   186→                targetLabel: target.label,
   187→                dialogue: decision.dialogue || '',
   188→                response: decision.targetDialogue || '',
   189→              });
   190→            }
   191→          }
   192→        }
   193→        break;
   194→      }
   195→    }
   196→
   197→    if (decision.dialogue) {
   198→      character.currentDialogue = decision.dialogue;
   199→      character.dialogueTimer   = 5000;
   200→    }
   201→
   202→    if (decision.description) {
   203→      console.log(`[${character.label}] ${decision.description}`);
   204→    }
   205→
   206→    if (this.onDecision) {
   207→      this.onDecision(character, decision, objects, simState);
   208→    }
   209→  }
   210→}
   211→

{"id":"599d44af-b81d-4b3e-bd50-5daf5c1132dd","body":"## Implementation complete — PR #5

### What was done

**`src/AIEngine.js`**
- `_requestDecision` now receives the full `characters` array and filters nearby characters (within 8 tiles, excluding self), then includes them in the prompt context as `{ name, label, tx, ty, action }`
- Added `talk` as a fourth action choice in the user prompt with `targetCharacter`, `dialogue`, and `targetDialogue` fields
- `_applyDecision` now handles `talk`: finds target by `name`, walks Character A to an adjacent walkable tile of Character B, sets Character B's `pendingSpeech` from `targetDialogue`, and pushes a `{ type: 'conversation', speakerLabel, targetLabel, dialogue, response }` event to the sim

**`src/Engine.js`**
- Added `pushEvent: (ev) => this.pendingEvents.push(ev)` to the `simState` object passed to `aiEngine.update()`, so the AI can append conversation events for the debug log

### Key decision
The AI response includes both `dialogue` (Character A's speech) and `targetDialogue` (Character B's scripted response). This keeps one round-trip per conversation and lets the LLM write both sides. Character B's `pendingSpeech` is set immediately when the decision applies — the speech bubble appears when the scene polls it, which naturally gives Character B time to \"hear\" A arrive.

{"id":"8ee40cbb-a2e5-43b1-b8a8-6c94ee3b9b3b","identifier":"FRG-206","title":"Bug: Characters never talk to each other","description":"AIEngine.\\_applyDecision only handles move/interact/idle — there is no talk action. Characters never approach each other for conversation.

## What exists

* AIEngine.\\_requestDecision builds a prompt with nearby objects, but NOT nearby characters
* The action choices in the prompt are: move, interact, idle
* Character has: currentDialogue, dialogueTimer, pendingSpeech properties
* SimulationEngine already handles pendingSpeech in its update loop

## Implementation

1. In AIEngine.\\_requestDecision: add nearby characters to the prompt context (name, position, current action)
2. Add 'talk' as a fourth action choice in the user prompt:
   { \"action\": \"talk\", \"targetCharacter\": \"character_name\", \"dialogue\": \"...\", \"description\": \"...\" }
3. In AIEngine.\\_applyDecision: add 'talk' case
   * Find target character by name
   * Walk Character A to adjacent tile of Character B (use findAdjacentWalkable)
   * Set Character A's dialogue
   * Set Character B's pendingSpeech to a contextual response (can be from the AI response or a simple acknowledgment)
4. Add conversation events to SimulationEngine.pendingEvents so the debug event log captures them

## Dependencies

* Depends on FRG-218 (AIEngine wired into debug page) to test on debug page
* Can be developed against main page first if needed

* AI prompt includes nearby characters as context
* Characters occasionally choose 'talk' action targeting another character
